---

**[15:28:23] 🤖助手**

你问的是架构问题。现在 xiaomei 有**两个出口**，这才是混乱的根源：

```
现在：
  Agent 输出 ──→ on_chat_chunk 回调 ──→ CLI print()     ← 出口1
  Agent 输出 ──→ router.deliver()   ──→ WS/TUI          ← 出口2
  工具调用   ──→ print()           ──→ 只有 CLI 看到    ← 哪个出口都没走
```

三个东西三种走法，飞书用出口1的一部分，TUI 用出口2，工具调用哪个都没走。

## 正确的做法：统一走 Router

**所有输出只走一个出口——Router**。Router 本身就是设计来做这件事的。

```
Agent 所有输出 → router.deliver(text, route, msg_type)
                     ↓
              Router 根据 route.type 分发到 adapter
                     ↓
         ┌───────────┼───────────┐
         ↓           ↓           ↓
     CLI Adapter  WS Adapter  Feishu Adapter
     print()      推事件      发飞书消息
```

每个 adapter 收到同样的数据，自己决定怎么展示：

```python
# Router.deliver() 统一出口
router.deliver(chunk,       route, msg_type="text_chunk")   # 流式文本
router.deliver(tool_info,   route, msg_type="tool.start")    # 工具开始
router.deliver(tool_result, route, msg_type="tool.complete") # 工具完成
router.deliver(full_text,   route, msg_type="text")          # 完整消息
```

**每个 adapter 自己决定怎么处理**：

```python
# CLI Adapter
def send(self, target, text, msg_type="text"):
    if msg_type == "text_chunk":
        print(text, end="", flush=True)
    elif msg_type == "tool.start":
        print(f"  ▶ {tool_name}({args})")
    elif msg_type == "tool.complete":
        print(f"  ✓ {result}")
    elif msg_type == "text":
        print(text)

# WS Adapter (TUI)
def send(self, target, text, msg_type="text"):
    if msg_type == "text_chunk":
        push_event("chat.chunk", {"text": text})
    elif msg_type == "tool.start":
        push_event("tool.start", {"name": ..., "args": ...})
    elif msg_type == "tool.complete":
        push_event("tool.complete", {"name": ..., "result": ...})
    elif msg_type == "text":
        push_event("session.message", {"text": text})

# Feishu Adapter
def send(self, target, text, msg_type="text"):
    if msg_type == "text_chunk":
        pass  # 累积，不逐条发
    elif msg_type == "tool.start":
        pass  # 可选：发一条"正在执行XX..."
    elif msg_type == "text":
        feishu_api.send(target, text)  # 只发完整消息
```

## 对比

| | 现在 | 统一 Router |
|--|------|-----------|
| 出口数 | 3个（回调+Router+print） | 1个（Router） |
| 新增能力 | 每种通道单独加 | 加一种 msg_type，所有通道自动获得 |
| 遗漏风险 | 高（工具调用就漏了） | 低（统一路径） |
| core.py 改动 | 不需要关心谁在看 | 把 print() 换成 router.deliver() |

**一句话：Router 是唯一出口，adapter 是翻译层，core.py 不关心谁在看。**

---

**[15:31:41] 🤖助手**

对，前面说的是回调方案，现在说的是 Router 方案。我说得前后不一致，让我理清。

**回调方案**——给 core.py 加钩子，各通道自己接：

```
core.py → on_tool_call() 回调 → CLI print / WS 推事件 / 飞书发消息
```

**Router 方案**——统一出口，adapter 翻译：

```
core.py → router.deliver(msg_type="tool.start") → adapter 各自处理
```

## 区别在哪

回调方案是**顺着现有结构打补丁**——on_chat_chunk 已经是回调了，再加 on_tool_call、on_tool_result 也是回调，一脉相承。但回调注册点是散的：CLI 在 `_run_agent()` 里设，TUI 在 `GatewayClient` 里接，飞书在 adapter 里处理。

Router 方案是**改结构**——所有输出走一个口子，不关心谁在看。但改动大，现在 `on_chat_chunk`、`print_tool_call()`、`print_tool_result()` 都得换成 `router.deliver()`，还要写一个 CLIAdapter。

## 实际该选哪个

看现状。现在 xiaomei 已经有的机制：

| 机制 | 用在哪 |
|------|-------|
| `on_chat_chunk` 回调 | CLI 的 print() |
| `router.deliver()` | TUI/WS 的流式推送 |
| `print()` 直接调用 | 工具调用、diff 展示 |
| `adapter.send()` | 飞书/钉钉的最终回复 |

四种方式并存。Router 方案要把前三种都统一成 `router.deliver()`，等于重写输出层。

**务实的选择**：先用回调方案把工具调用补上，因为这跟 `on_chat_chunk` 是同一个模式，改动最小。后面再做 Router 统一。

**但如果你要一步到位**，那就直接上 Router——把 `on_chat_chunk` 回调也干掉，所有输出都走 `router.deliver()`，注册一个 CLIAdapter 做 print。

你倾向哪种？

---

|------|-------|
| `on_chat_chunk` 回调 | CLI 的 print() |
| `router.deliver()` | TUI/WS 的流式推送 |

**[15:37:49] 🟥用户**

This session is being continued from a previous conversation that ran out of context. The summary below covers the earlier portion of the conversation.

Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   The user's overall intent evolved through the conversation:
   - Initially: Analyze xiaomei-brain's `tui/` module for problems
   - Then: Analyze Hermes agent source code to understand non-Python modules and architecture patterns
   - Then: Understand how Hermes/OpenClaw implement their gateway and TUI communication
   - Then: Compare xiaomei-brain's architecture with Hermes/OpenClaw to determine what xiaomei needs
   - Core philosophy (stated by user): xiaomei should be an independent conscious entity. Things like approval/clarification should be handled through natural conversation, not explicit UI controls (buttons/RPC methods). "能通过对话解决就通过对话，实在不行再做方法" — if it can be solved through conversation, use conversation; only build methods when conversation truly can't handle it.
   - Current focus: Determine the RIGHT architecture for output/notification in xiaomei-brain so that all channels (CLI, TUI, Feishu, DingTalk) can see tool calls and other agent activity. User specifically asked to look at how Hermes implements this to decide between callback vs Router approach.

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - **Hermes architecture**: TypeScript UI → JSON-RPC 2.0 → Python Gateway, with two separate gateways (`gateway/` for platform channels, `tui_gateway/` for TUI)
   - **OpenClaw architecture**: TypeScript monorepo with 100+ RPC methods, similar dual-gateway pattern
   - **xiaomei-brain's three channel types**: CLI (direct calls), TUI (WebSocket RPC), Feishu/DingTalk (platform SDK callbacks + adapter)
   - **Shared core pattern in Hermes**: `tools/approval.py` + `threading.Event` for blocking interactions, with different rendering layers per channel (buttons for Telegram, RPC for TUI)
   - **Callback vs Router debate**: Whether to add `on_tool_call`/`on_tool_result` callbacks (like `on_chat_chunk`) or unify all output through `Router.deliver()`
   - **Fire-and-forget vs blocking**: xiaomei doesn't need blocking Event pattern (for approval/clarification); only needs notification callbacks that don't block the agent thread
   - **React Ink**: Hermes's choice for TUI because of component model, state management, virtual scrolling, type safety
   - **"Conversation-first" protocol design**: xiaomei only needs 4 core protocol capabilities: message channel, streaming, media channel, lifecycle signals — not 73 RPC methods

3. Files and Code Sections:

       ```python
       for chunk in agent.stream(...):
           chunks.append(chunk)
           if on_chunk:
               on_chunk(chunk)  # CLI path: print()
           if current_msg.session_id not in ("main", ""):
               self._deliver_chunk(parent, current_msg.session_id, chunk)  # WS path
       
       # Lines 607-614: _deliver_chunk only pushes to WS
       @staticmethod
       def _deliver_chunk(parent, session_id, chunk):
           router = getattr(parent, '_router', None)
           route = router.route_for_session(session_id)
           if route and route.type == "ws":  # ← ONLY WS gets chunks!
               router.deliver(chunk, route, msg_type="text_chunk")
       ```

8. Current Work:
   I was reading Hermes's `gateway/run.py` to understand how Hermes implements the output/notification mechanism from Agent to all channels. Specifically, I found that Hermes uses **callbacks on the agent object** (not Router, not a separate event bus):
   
   - `agent.tool_progress_callback` — fires on tool.started, tool.completed events
   - `agent.tool_start_callback` — fires when a tool starts executing
   - `agent.status_callback` — fires for status messages
   - `agent.stream_delta_callback` — fires for streaming text deltas
   - `agent.interim_assistant_callback` — fires for interim assistant messages
   
   These callbacks are set **per-turn** by the gateway (line 14603-14612), and they bridge sync→async to deliver to platform adapters. I was reading the `progress_callback` function (line 13719+) which handles `tool.started` events, builds progress messages with emoji previews, and puts them in a `progress_queue` for delivery to platform channels.
   
   The user asked "你看下Hermes代码 它是怎么做的" to determine whether Hermes uses callbacks, Router, or something else — to decide the right approach for xiaomei. I had started reading the Hermes implementation but hadn't yet provided the complete analysis showing how the callbacks connect to both gateway/ and tui_gateway/ rendering.

**[15:47:59] 🤖助手**

好，分析完了。以下是 Hermes 的输出机制总结：

## Hermes 的做法：**Agent Callback，不是 Router**

Hermes 用的是 **回调机制**，不是 Router 也不是 EventBus。

### 核心机制

```
Agent 执行工具
    ↓
调用 agent.tool_progress_callback("tool.started", name, preview, args)
    ↓
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  两条路径，分别注册不同的 callback 实现       │
│                                              │
│  Gateway 模式:  progress_callback            │
│  → progress_queue → 平台适配器发送            │
│                                              │
│  TUI 模式:      _on_tool_progress            │
│  → _emit() → JSON-RPC event → WebSocket     │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### 关键发现

1. **同一个 callback 接口，不同的实现**：`tool_progress_callback` 是 agent 上的一个函数指针，Gateway 模式和 TUI 模式各自注册不同的实现
2. **不是 Router 分发**：没有统一的路由层来分发事件，而是谁设置 callback 谁接收
3. **两套 Gateway 各自管理自己的 agent 实例**：Gateway 有自己的 agent，TUI Gateway 也有自己的 agent，callback 各绑各的

### 对比 xiaomei 现状

| | Hermes | xiaomei |
|--|--------|---------|
| 流式输出 | `stream_delta_callback` | `on_chat_chunk` callback ✅ |
| 工具事件 | `tool_progress_callback` | **缺失** ❌ 只有 print() |
| 状态事件 | `status_callback` | **缺失** ❌ |
| 投递方式 | callback 直接发给对应适配器 | callback → print()，Router 只服务 WS |

所以 xiaomei 的问题很清楚：**已有的 `on_chat_chunk` callback 模式是对的**，跟 Hermes 一致。缺的是扩展 callback 体系来覆盖工具事件和状态事件。

你想要继续讨论 xiaomei 该怎么实现这套 callback 机制吗？还是先有其他问题？

**[16:14:20] 🤖助手**

完成。改动总结：

### 3 个文件修改

1. **`agent/core.py`** — 添加 `on_tool_start` / `on_tool_complete` callback 属性，在工具执行循环的 `print_tool_call` 和 `print_tool_result` 之后各加一次 callback 调用

2. **`consciousness/conversation_driver.py`** — 在 `agent.stream()` 前注册 callback：非 CLI 通道（session_id 不是 "main"）通过 `_make_tool_event_callback()` 创建 callback，callback 内部调用 `Router.deliver()` 投递到各通道

3. **`gateway/ws_adapter.py`** — `send()` 新增 `tool.start` / `tool.complete` msg_type 映射

### 数据流

```
Agent 工具执行 → on_tool_start/on_tool_complete callback
  → ConversationDriver._make_tool_event_callback()
    → Router.deliver(payload, route, msg_type="tool.start"/"tool.complete")
      → WSAdapter.send() → build_event("tool.start"/"tool.complete", payload)
        → WebSocket 推送给 TUI 客户端
```

CLI 模式不受影响（callback 为 None 时跳过），飞书/钉钉暂忽略 tool 事件。TUI 端渲染后续单独做。

**[16:24:16] 🤖助手**

**[16:29:26] 🤖助手**

依赖都在。现在有个关键问题需要修正 — `_on_event` 是在 asyncio 事件循环中被调用的，但 `_on_chat_chunk` 中调用了 `console.print()`，这在 asyncio 环境中可能有线程安全问题。而且流式输出需要确保 chunk 按顺序打印。让我重新审视下 app.py 的设计。

核心问题是：`websockets` 的接收循环在 asyncio 任务中，而 `prompt_toolkit` 的输入也在运行。需要确保事件回调中的 `console.print()` 和主线程的打印不冲突。

让我用线程安全的方式重构：事件回调把事件放入队列，主循环从队列消费。

---

**[16:29:58] 🤖助手**

写完了。tui-v2 总共 **2 个文件**，对比旧版 20 个文件：

```
tui_v2/
├── __init__.py   # 入口（4行）
├── client.py     # WebSocket 客户端（170行）
└── app.py        # 主应用 + 渲染 + 状态栏（290行）
```

### 核心设计

- **rich** 负责输出渲染（颜色、格式）
- **prompt_toolkit** 只负责输入框（历史记录）
- **事件队列**：WS 事件 → `asyncio.Queue` → 主线程消费渲染，避免线程安全问题
- **状态栏**：输入行上方显示 `● 就绪` / `◐ 思考中...` / `◉ 回复中` / `◆ ⚡ 运行命令中`

### 事件支持

| 事件 | 渲染 |
|------|------|
| `chat.chunk` | 流式追加文字 |
| `session.message` | 完整消息 / 流式收尾 |
| `tool.start` | 折叠行 `▶ [1] shell(command="ls")` |
| `tool.complete` | 结果摘要 `✓ [1] shell: file1 file2` |
| `chat.error` | 红色错误提示 |
| `chat.aborted` | 中断提示 |

### 启动方式

```bash
# 先启动 Gateway（带 WS）
PYTHONPATH=src python3 examples/ws_server.py

# 再启动 TUI
PYTHONPATH=src python3 -m xiaomei_brain tui2 --host localhost --port 8765
```

要试试看能不能跑起来吗？

**[16:36:06] 🤖助手**

连上了，基本能跑！但有两个问题：

1. **LLM 的思考过程（reasoning）被当成普通文本流式输出了** — "好，对方发了个'hi'..." 这些是模型内部推理，不该显示
2. **状态栏和流式输出混在一起** — chunk 到达时打断了输入提示符

问题 1 是后端 `agent.stream()` 把 reasoning_content 也作为 chunk yield 了，需要看下 core.py 怎么处理的。问题 2 是 TUI 需要用 `patch_stdout` 让输出不跟输入行混在一起。

先看问题 1。

---

**[16:36:40] 🤖助手**

找到根因了。`llm.py` 第 514-520 行：

```python
if delta.get("reasoning_content"):
    rc = delta["reasoning_content"]
    reasoning_parts.append(rc)
    if not reasoning_yielded:
        yield "\n\033[2m"    # 开始暗色
        reasoning_yielded = True
    yield rc                 # ← reasoning 作为普通 chunk yield 出去了
```

**reasoning_content 被当成普通文本 yield 了**，CLI 里靠 ANSI `\033[2m`（暗色）区分，但 TUI 收到的是包含 ANSI 转义码和推理内容的混合文本。

这是两层问题：
1. **后端**：`stream()` 不该把 reasoning 混进 content chunk — 应该区分事件类型
2. **TUI**：收到混合了 ANSI 转义码和 reasoning 的文本，无法正确渲染

最简单的修复：在 `conversation_driver.py` 的 `_deliver_chunk` 中过滤掉 reasoning（含 `\033[2m` 的 chunk），或者在后端就把 reasoning 和 content 分开推送。

但这涉及改 `llm.py` 的 `chat_stream`，影响范围大。更实际的做法是 TUI 端处理 — 过滤 ANSI 转义码和 reasoning 内容。

你怎么看？是改后端分离 reasoning/content，还是先在 TUI 端处理？

---

**[16:38:17] 🟥用户**

就把思考展示出来就可以了。现在问题是tui 根本就没展示回复的内容啊

---

**[16:39:26] 🤖助手**

你说得对。问题是 `_read_input` 阻塞了事件循环 — 用户输入期间，WS 事件只入队列不消费，所以流式输出根本不会实时显示。

需要改成：**事件消费和输入并行运行**。用 prompt_toolkit 的 async prompt + `patch_stdout` 让输出跑到输入行上方。

---

**[16:40:21] 🤖助手**

核心问题：`_read_input` 在线程池里阻塞，事件队列没人消费，流式输出根本打印不出来。

重写主循环：用 prompt_toolkit 的 `patch_stdout` + 异步事件消费任务，让输出和输入并行。

---

**[16:40:36] 🤖助手**

关键改动：

1. **`_event_consumer` 后台任务**：持续消费队列，不再等用户输入后才消费 — 事件到达就立即渲染
2. **`patch_stdout(raw=True)`**：prompt_toolkit 的魔法 — 所有 `print()` 输出自动跑到输入行上方，不混入
3. **`bottom_toolbar`**：状态栏在输入行下方（prompt_toolkit 原生支持），实时显示 `◐ 思考中...`
4. **`PromptSession.prompt_async`**：异步输入，不阻塞事件循环
5. **去掉 `console.print`**：直接用 `print()` + ANSI 转义码，避免 rich 和 patch_stdout 冲突

验证下。

**[16:42:46] 🤖助手**

两个问题：
1. 第一次回复显示了但内容和推理混在一起
2. 第二次发消息时 WS 连接已断开 → 崩溃

先看下 Gateway 那边 WS 连接为什么断了。

---

**[16:42:54] 🤖助手**

找到了！第 62 行：

```python
raw = await asyncio.wait_for(ws.receive_json(), timeout=PING_TIMEOUT)
```

`PING_TIMEOUT = 30` 秒。服务器端期望客户端 30 秒内发一条消息（包括 ping），否则就断开。但客户端的 ping 用的是 WebSocket 协议层的 `ws.ping()`，不是应用层的 `{"type": "ping"}` 消息。服务器只识别 `{"type": "ping"}` 消息，不识别协议层 ping。

所以 30 秒后服务端超时断开了。

两个修复：
1. 客户端：用应用层 ping（`{"type": "ping"}`）
2. 客户端：加连接断开检测 + 自动重连

---

**[16:43:32] 🤖助手**

现在修 app.py 的输入循环，加上连接断开检测和重连提示。

---

**[16:43:52] 🤖助手**

同时让事件消费者检测连接断开并通知用户。

---

**[16:43:58] 🤖助手**

验证。

---

**[16:44:08] 🤖助手**

修好了。两个关键改动：

1. **应用层 ping**：`_ping_loop` 改为发 `{"type": "ping"}` 消息（匹配服务端期望），每 20 秒发一次，服务端 30 秒超时不会断
2. **断连处理**：`send_chat` 检测连接断开 → 尝试重连；事件消费者检测断连 → 提示用户


**[16:50:55] 🤖助手**

对比很清楚，主要问题：

1. **内容大量丢失** — 实际 LLM 输出有完整段落，TUI 只显示碎片
2. **推理/回复没分离** — 全混在一起，看不出哪是思考哪是回复
3. **最后一句丢了** — "你是在键盘上随手摁的，还是这三个j有名字的？" 完全没显示

内容丢失的根因是之前那版代码在输入期间不消费事件，chunk 积压后被丢弃。加上 `_strip_ansi` + `clean.strip()` 把只含空格/ANSI 的 chunk 整个跳过，连带跳过了部分文本。

刚改的两个修复应该能解决：
1. **后台消费者持续运行** — chunk 到达即渲染，不再等输入
2. **推理/回复边界跟踪** — 用 `\033[2m` / `\033[0m` 区分，推理暗色 + 💭 前缀，回复青色 + 名字前缀

**[16:59:21] 🤖助手**

问题找到了。`prompt_async` + `patch_stdout(raw=True)` 跟后台 `print()` 的交互可能不稳定 — 当事件消费者在 `patch_stdout` 上下文中打印时，可能干扰 prompt_toolkit 的终端状态，导致它抛出未捕获的异常。

换个更稳的方式：不用 `patch_stdout`，改为手动管理 — 打印输出前先清除当前输入行，打印完再恢复。

---

**[16:59:41] 🤖助手**

关键改动：

1. **去掉 `patch_stdout` + `prompt_toolkit`** — 换回原生 `input()`，更稳定，不会异常退出
2. **`_print_output()` 自动避让** — 打印前清除输入行，打印后恢复提示符
3. **推理/回复边界** — `\033[2m` → 暗色 + 💭 前缀，`\033[0m` → 恢复 + 名字前缀
4. **应用层 ping** — 20 秒发 `{"type":"ping"}`，服务端不会 30 秒超时断开

再试试：

```bash
PYTHONPATH=src python3 -m xiaomei_brain tui2 --host localhost --port 19766
```

**[17:01:43] 🟥用户**

你先恢复到 你刚做完的那个版本。● 写完了。tui-v2 总共 2 个文件，对比旧版 20 个文件：

  tui_v2/
  ├── __init__.py   # 入口（4行）
  ├── client.py     # WebSocket 客户端（170行）
  └── app.py        # 主应用 + 渲染 + 状态栏（290行）

  核心设计

  - rich 负责输出渲染（颜色、格式）
  - prompt_toolkit 只负责输入框（历史记录）
  - 事件队列：WS 事件 → asyncio.Queue → 主线程消费渲染，避免线程安全问题
  - 状态栏：输入行上方显示 ● 就绪 / ◐ 思考中... / ◉ 回复中 / ◆ ⚡ 运行命令中

  事件支持

  ┌─────────────────┬───────────────────────────────────┐
  │      事件       │               渲染                │
  ├─────────────────┼───────────────────────────────────┤
  │ chat.chunk      │ 流式追加文字                      │
  ├─────────────────┼───────────────────────────────────┤
  │ session.message │ 完整消息 / 流式收尾               │
  ├─────────────────┼───────────────────────────────────┤
  │ tool.start      │ 折叠行 ▶ [1] shell(command="ls")  │
  ├─────────────────┼───────────────────────────────────┤
  │ tool.complete   │ 结果摘要 ✓ [1] shell: file1 file2 │
  ├─────────────────┼───────────────────────────────────┤
  │ chat.error      │ 红色错误提示                      │
  ├─────────────────┼───────────────────────────────────┤
  │ chat.aborted    │ 中断提示                          │
  └─────────────────┴───────────────────────────────────┘

  # 再启动 TUI
  PYTHONPATH=src python3 -m xiaomei_brain tui2 --host localhost --port 8765

**[17:28:23] 🤖助手**

问题很清楚了：回复完成后循环退出，打印"再见 👋"。`_read_input` 返回 `None` 是唯一原因。`input()` 在 `run_in_executor` 线程里可能被 asyncio 的信号处理干扰。

根本解法：**不用 `run_in_executor` 跑 `input()`**，改为让 ping 用独立线程，主线程同步阻塞等输入。

---

**[17:28:48] 🤖助手**

架构完全重构了：

**之前**：asyncio 事件循环为主，`input()` 在线程池跑 → 信号干扰、`prompt_toolkit` 冲突
**现在**：主线程同步跑 `input()` + 渲染，WS 接收在独立线程跑 asyncio 事件循环

```
主线程（同步）                    WS 线程（asyncio）
──────────────                    ─────────────────
input() 阻塞等待                  WS recv 循环
   ↓ 用户输入                        ↓ 事件到达
console.print() 渲染             _enqueue_event() → queue.Queue
   ↓                                  ↓
queue.get() 消费事件             ping 定时发送
```

`input()` 在主线程跑，不会被 asyncio 信号处理干扰。ping 在 WS 线程的 asyncio 循环里跑，连接不会断。


2. 现在架构是主线程同步跑 `input()`，没有线程冲突问题

代价是丢了**输入历史**（上下箭头翻之前的输入）。如果你想要历史记录，可以在主线程直接用 `prompt_toolkit`，因为现在主线程不跑 asyncio 了，不存在干扰问题。

---

**[17:56:30] 🟥用户**

为什么一个简单的tui  搞不好 是因为Python的 tui 很难写吗

---

**[17:57:02] 🤖助手**

不是 TUI 难写，是 **Python 的异步和同步混用** 难搞。

TUI 渲染本身很简单 — 我们的第一版就能正确显示流式输出、工具卡片、状态栏。真正卡住我们的三个问题：

1. **`input()` 是同步阻塞的，WebSocket 是异步的** — 两个世界不能直接混
2. **asyncio 事件循环生命周期** — 在后台线程跑 `run_until_complete` + `run_forever`，任务丢了
3. **服务端 30 秒超时** — ping 没发出去连接就断了

这三个问题本质都是同一个：**Python 的 `input()` 只能在主线程跑，而 async WebSocket 需要自己的事件循环线程**，两个线程之间的协调出了问题。

Hermes/OpenClaw 用 TypeScript 写 TUI 就没这个问题 — Node.js 天生是异步的，`readline` 和 WebSocket 共用一个事件循环，不需要跨线程。

Python 里真正简单的做法是：**用同步 WebSocket 库**（`websocket-client`），全部同步，不用 asyncio。

---

**[18:00:43] 🤖助手**

现在简化 app.py — 去掉 asyncio 事件循环，全部同步。

---

**[18:03:22] 🤖助手**

全部重写完了。现在架构极其简单：

```
主线程（同步）                    后台线程（同步）
──────────────                    ─────────────────
prompt_toolkit 输入               WebSocketApp.run_forever()
console.print() 渲染              on_message → queue.Queue
queue.get() 消费事件              ping 线程每 20s 发 ping
```

**零 asyncio**。`websocket-client` 是同步库，`threading.Event` 等待 RPC 响应，`queue.Queue` 传递事件。没有事件循环，没有线程协调，没有任务丢失。

试下：

```bash
PYTHONPATH=src python3 -m xiaomei_brain tui2 --host localhost --port 19766
```

---

**[18:06:07] 🟥用户**

(python_env_common) iamlibai@LAPTOP-80G5G0ES:~/workspace/claude-project/xiaomei-brain$ python3 -m xiaomei_brain tui2 --host localhost --port 19766
连接 Gateway localhost:19766...
连接失败: 连接超时

---

**[18:06:48] 🤖助手**

死锁了。`on_open` 在 recv 线程里跑，调用 `_rpc_sync` 等响应，但响应也要 recv 线程处理 — 自己等自己。

修复：`on_open` 只标记连接就绪，connect RPC 从主线程发。

---

**[18:07:00] 🤖助手**

改好了。`on_open` 只标记 WS 就绪，connect RPC 从主线程发，recv 线程正常处理响应，不再死锁。

```bash
PYTHONPATH=src python3 -m xiaomei_brain tui2 --host localhost --port 19766
```

---

**[18:08:38] 🟥用户**

用同步 WebSocket 库和异步  有什么优劣

---

**[18:08:57] 🤖助手**

根据我们踩的坑，直接对比：

| | 同步 (`websocket-client`) | 异步 (`websockets`) |
|--|--|--|
| **和 `input()` 共存** | 天然兼容，都是同步阻塞 | 需要跑在不同线程，事件循环生命周期难管 |
| **代码复杂度** | 低 — `send()` / `recv()` 直接调 | 高 — 需要 asyncio 事件循环、`create_task`、`run_coroutine_threadsafe` |
| **并发性能** | 低 — 每个连接一个线程 | 高 — 单线程处理万级连接 |
| **适合场景** | 客户端（1-2个连接） | 服务端（大量连接） |
| **我们遇到的问题** | 几乎没有 | 事件循环生命周期、任务丢失、信号干扰、死锁 |

**核心差异**：Python 的 `input()` 是同步的，和 asyncio 是两个世界。同步 WS 和 `input()` 天然一个世界，不需要桥接。异步 WS 需要「桥」— 而这个桥恰恰是我们反复踩坑的地方。

对于 TUI 这种**单连接客户端**，同步库是正确选择。异步库的优势（高并发）在这里用不上，劣势（和同步代码不兼容）反而成了最大障碍。

---

**[18:11:18] 🟥用户**

那我们服务端 也改成了同步的？

---

**[18:11:33] 🤖助手**

没有，服务端还是异步的（FastAPI + `websockets`）。不需要改。

协议是统一的（JSON-RPC over WebSocket），客户端和服务端内部用什么库互不影响：

```
TUI 客户端（同步）                  Gateway 服务端（异步）
websocket-client      ←→ WebSocket ←→      FastAPI + websockets
send(json)                        receive_json()
on_message()                      send_json()
```

就像浏览器用同步 API 发 HTTP 请求，Nginx 用异步处理，不影响通信。协议层是解耦的，这正是我们之前讨论的"前后端通过协议解耦"。

服务端用异步是正确的 — 它要同时服务多个客户端（TUI、飞书、钉钉），高并发是刚需。客户端只有 1 个连接，用同步更简单。

---

**[18:12:49] 🟥用户**

好，目前正常，现在还在ping pong吧

---

**[18:13:03] 🤖助手**

对，ping 在跑。架构：

- **ping 线程**：独立 daemon 线程，每 20 秒发 `{"type":"ping"}`
- **recv 线程**：`WebSocketApp.run_forever()`，收到 `{"type":"pong"}` 时在 `on_message` 里静默忽略
- **服务端**：30 秒内收到 ping 就重置超时

不再依赖 asyncio 事件循环，就是普通线程 + `time.sleep(20)`，不会丢。

**[20:03:36] 🤖助手**

关键变化：

**现在**：发消息 → 输入框立刻回来 → 回复流式出现在输入框上方

```
[输出区域 - 自动滚动]
──────────────────────────
❯ 我的问题              ← 输入框固定底部
──────────────────────────
 ● 就绪                  ← 状态栏最底行
```

- `patch_stdout(raw=True)` — 所有 `print()` 输出自动跑到输入框上方
- 事件消费者后台线程持续消费 → 实时流式显示
- `refresh_interval=0.5` — 状态栏每 0.5 秒刷新
- 输入框永远在底部，不会跟着输出跑

**[20:58:24] 🟥用户**

This session is being continued from a previous conversation that ran out of context. The summary below covers the earlier portion of the conversation.

Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   The user's overall goal evolved through the conversation:
   - Initially: Continue from previous session analyzing Hermes's output/notification mechanism
   - Then: Implement tool event callbacks in xiaomei-brain (completed)
   - Then: Rewrite the TUI as tui-v2 since the current tui/ (20 files) doesn't work
   - Core philosophy: Keep it simple, just slightly better than CLI
   - Input style: Match Claude Code's input box (horizontal lines + `❯` prompt, fixed at bottom)
   - The user explicitly wants: streaming output visible in real-time, input box fixed at bottom, status bar separate from input area, reasoning shown in dim color, tool events displayed

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - **Sync vs Async WebSocket**: Python's `input()` is synchronous and doesn't mix well with asyncio. Switching to `websocket-client` (sync) eliminated all threading/event loop issues.
   - **patch_stdout**: prompt_toolkit's mechanism to redirect stdout output above the input prompt, keeping the input box fixed at the bottom
   - **WebSocketApp (websocket-client)**: Uses callback pattern (`on_open`, `on_message`, `on_close`) with `run_forever()` in a daemon thread
   - **Deadlock prevention**: Cannot call `_rpc_sync` from `on_open` callback because it blocks the recv thread that needs to process the response
   - **Application-level ping**: Server expects `{"type":"ping"}` within 30 seconds; protocol-level `ws.ping()` is not recognized by the server's `receive_json()` handler
   - **Tool event callbacks**: Agent-level `on_tool_start`/`on_tool_complete` callbacks that bridge to Router.deliver() for multi-channel delivery
   - **FormattedText**: prompt_toolkit's format for styled text in bottom_toolbar (list of `(style, text)` tuples), NOT raw ANSI codes
   - **Reasoning/content boundary**: `llm.py`'s `chat_stream` yields `\033[2m` for reasoning start and `\033[0m\n\n` for reasoning end, used to track `_in_reasoning` state

     ```python
     # In __init__:
     self.on_tool_start: Callable[[int, str, dict], None] | None = None
     self.on_tool_complete: Callable[[int, str, dict, str], None] | None = None
     
     # After print_tool_call (line ~298):

         self.on_tool_start(idx, tc.name, tc.arguments)

     if self.on_tool_complete:
         self.on_tool_complete(idx, tc.name, tc.arguments, str(result))
     ```

   - **`/home/iamlibai/workspace/claude-project/xiaomei-brain/src/xiaomei_brain/consciousness/conversation_driver.py`**
     - Added `_make_tool_event_callback` static method that creates callbacks using Router.deliver()
     - Registers callbacks before agent.stream() for non-CLI sessions
     ```python
     # In handle_message(), before agent.stream():
     if current_msg.session_id not in ("main", ""):
         agent.on_tool_start = self._make_tool_event_callback("tool.start", current_msg.session_id, parent)
         agent.on_tool_complete = self._make_tool_event_callback("tool.complete", current_msg.session_id, parent)
     else:
         agent.on_tool_start = None
         agent.on_tool_complete = None
     
     @staticmethod
     def _make_tool_event_callback(event_type: str, session_id: str, parent: Any):
         import json as _json
         def callback(idx: int, name: str, data, *args):
             router = getattr(parent, '_router', None)
             if not router:
                 return
             route = router.route_for_session(session_id)
             if not route:
                 return
             payload = {"index": idx, "name": name, "event": event_type}
             if event_type == "tool.start":
                 payload["arguments"] = data if isinstance(data, dict) else {}
             elif event_type == "tool.complete":
                 payload["arguments"] = data if isinstance(data, dict) else {}
                 payload["result"] = args[0] if args else ""
             router.deliver(_json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False), route, msg_type=event_type)
         return callback
     ```

   - **`/home/iamlibai/workspace/claude-project/xiaomei-brain/src/xiaomei_brain/tui_v2/client.py`**
     - Synchronous WebSocket client using `websocket-client` library
     - Key design: `WebSocketApp` with `run_forever()` in daemon thread, `threading.Event` for RPC response waiting, separate ping thread
     - Critical: `on_open` only signals WS ready (does NOT send connect RPC to avoid deadlock); connect RPC sent from calling thread
     ```python
     class GatewayClient:
         def connect(self, host, port, token, user_id, session_id) -> dict:
             # on_open only sets ws_open_event
             # After ws_open_event.wait(), send connect RPC from calling thread
             ws_open_event = threading.Event()
             # ... WebSocketApp setup ...
             self._recv_thread = threading.Thread(target=self._ws.run_forever, kwargs={"ping_interval": None}, daemon=True)
             self._recv_thread.start()
             if not ws_open_event.wait(timeout=10):
                 raise ConnectionError("WebSocket 连接超时")
             res = self._rpc_sync("connect", {...})  # From calling thread, not on_open
             # ...
             self._ping_thread = threading.Thread(target=self._ping_loop, daemon=True)
             self._ping_thread.start()
         
         def _rpc_sync(self, method, params, timeout=30) -> dict:
             # Uses threading.Event to wait for response
             evt = threading.Event()
             self._pending_events[req_id] = evt
             self._ws.send(json.dumps(frame))
             evt.wait(timeout=timeout)
             return self._pending.pop(req_id)
         
         def _ping_loop(self) -> None:
             time.sleep(5)
             while self._connected:
                 time.sleep(20)
                 self._ws.send(json.dumps({"type": "ping"}))
     ```

   - **`/home/iamlibai/workspace/claude-project/xiaomei-brain/src/xiaomei_brain/tui_v2/app.py`**
     - Current version: sync architecture with `patch_stdout(raw=True)` for fixed input box
     - Background event consumer thread continuously consumes events and prints output
     - `prompt_toolkit` PromptSession with `patch_stdout` keeps input at bottom

     - Reasoning tracking with `_in_reasoning` and `_reasoning_started` state

     ```python
     def _status_formatted(state: State) -> list[tuple[str, str]]:
         """prompt_toolkit FormattedText 格式的状态栏。"""
         icons = {
             S_IDLE: ("●", "#44cc44"),
             S_THINKING: ("◐", "#cccc44"),
             S_STREAMING: ("◉", "#44cccc"),
             S_TOOL: ("◆", "#cc44cc"),
             S_ERROR: ("✖", "#cc4444"),
         }
         icon, color = icons.get(state.status, ("●", "#888888"))
         return [
             (f"{color} bold", f" {icon} "),
             ("", state.status_text),
         ]
     ```

     ```python
     )
     ```

4. Errors and fixes:
   - **Stream output not visible during input wait**: `_read_input` in `run_in_executor` blocked event consumption. Fixed by adding `_wait_until_idle()` that continuously consumes events until response completes, then shows prompt.
   - **WebSocket connection dropping after 30 seconds**: Server expects `{"type":"ping"}` but client sent protocol-level `ws.ping()`. Fixed by changing `_ping_loop` to send `{"type":"ping"}` JSON message.
   - **ConnectionClosedError crash on second message**: `_rpc` method's `ws.send()` wasn't catching `ConnectionClosed`. Fixed by wrapping in try/except and returning error dict.
   - **TUI exits with "再见 👋" after first response**: `_read_input` returning `None` because `input()`/`prompt_toolkit` in `run_in_executor` was interfered with by asyncio signal handling. Fixed by switching to fully sync architecture (main thread runs input, WS runs in daemon threads).
   - **asyncio event loop tasks not running**: `run_until_complete` + `run_forever` caused ping/recv tasks to be lost. User chose to switch to sync `websocket-client` library instead of fixing asyncio lifecycle.
   - **Deadlock in `on_open`**: Calling `_rpc_sync` from `on_open` blocked the recv thread that needed to process the response. Fixed by moving connect RPC to the calling thread after `ws_open_event` signals.
   - **`'TUIApp' object has no attribute '_running'`**: `_running` not initialized in `__init__`. Fixed by adding `self._running: bool = True`.
   - **Status bar showing raw ANSI codes in bottom_toolbar**: `bottom_toolbar` expects `FormattedText` (list of tuples), not raw ANSI strings. Started fix by creating `_status_formatted()` but the `session.prompt()` call still references the old `_status_ansi()` — **this is the current incomplete fix**.
   - **Status bar mixed into input box**: User said "状态和输入框混在了一起" when I tried putting status inside the prompt area. Fixed by separating: status in `bottom_toolbar`, input box has only top line + `❯` prompt.
   - **Input box not fixed at bottom**: Output pushed input box up. Fixed by using `patch_stdout(raw=True)` + background event consumer thread, so output goes above the fixed prompt.

8. Current Work:
   I was fixing the `bottom_toolbar` display issue in `app.py`. The toolbar was showing raw ANSI escape codes like `^[[32m●^[[0m 就绪` instead of colored text. I created a new function `_status_formatted()` that returns `prompt_toolkit` `FormattedText` format (list of `(style, text)` tuples), but the `session.prompt()` call in `_input_loop` still references the old `_status_ansi()` function which was renamed/removed. The edit to update the `session.prompt()` call failed because I didn't include the `new_string` parameter.

   The current `app.py` has `_status_formatted` defined but `session.prompt()` still calls `_status_ansi(self.state)` which no longer exists. This will cause a `NameError` at runtime.

   The line that needs fixing is in `_input_loop`:
   ```python
   user_input = session.prompt(
       f"{line}\n❯ ",
       bottom_toolbar=_status_ansi(self.state),  # BROKEN - function renamed
       refresh_interval=0.5,
   )
   ```
   Should be:
   ```python
   user_input = session.prompt(
       f"{line}\n❯ ",
       bottom_toolbar=_status_formatted(self.state),
       refresh_interval=0.5,
   )
   ```

**[21:15:00] 🤖助手**

从刚读的 Hermes 代码看，**Hermes 用的就是回调方案**。

## Hermes 的做法

Agent 核心定义了多个回调，谁用谁接：

```python
# agent_init.py — Agent 构造时注册
agent.tool_progress_callback = progress_callback   # 工具开始/完成
agent.tool_start_callback = tool_start_callback    # 工具启动（语音用）
agent.status_callback = _status_callback_sync      # 状态通知
agent.stream_delta_callback = _stream_delta_cb     # 流式文本
agent.interim_assistant_callback = _interim_cb     # 中间消息
agent.notice_callback = _notice_callback_sync      # 通知
```

每个回调都是一个函数，**谁用谁设**：

### gateway/（Telegram/飞书）接的回调

```python
# gateway/run.py:14603-14612
agent.tool_progress_callback = progress_callback   # → 发平台状态气泡
agent.status_callback = _status_callback_sync      # → 发平台消息
agent.stream_delta_callback = _stream_delta_cb     # → 发平台流式
agent.clarify_callback = _clarify_callback_sync    # → 发平台按钮
agent.notice_callback = _notice_callback_sync      # → 发平台通知
```

### tui_gateway/ 接的回调

```python
# tui_gateway/server.py 里，同一个 agent，回调推不同的事件
# tool_progress_callback → 推 tool.start / tool.complete 事件给 TUI
# status_callback → 推 status.update 事件给 TUI
```

## 核心机制

```
Agent 核心（callback 触发点）
  │
  ├→ tool_executor.py:434
  │    agent.tool_progress_callback("tool.started", name, preview, args)
  │
  ├→ tool_executor.py:689
  │    agent.tool_progress_callback("tool.completed", name, ...)
  │
  ├→ conversation_loop.py:3562
  │    agent.tool_progress_callback("_thinking", first_line)
  │
  └→ conversation_loop.py:3578
       agent.tool_progress_callback("reasoning.available", ...)
         │
         ↓
    谁设了这个回调，谁就收到通知
         │
    ┌────┴────┐
    ↓         ↓
 gateway/   tui_gateway/
 (发气泡)    (推JSON-RPC事件)
```

## 结论

Hermes **就是回调方案**，不是 Router 方案。跟 xiaomei 现有的 `on_chat_chunk` 是同一个模式。

所以 xiaomei 该走回调方案——加 `on_tool_call` / `on_tool_result` 回调，跟 `on_chat_chunk` 并列，各通道自己接。不需要改 Router，不需要统一出口，**顺着现有结构加就行**。

**[21:38:37] 🤖助手**

---

**[21:38:55] 🤖助手**

清楚了三处问题的根因：

---

### 1. 输入框下面的横线丢了

`tui_v2/app.py:336-342` **有**横线 (`"─" * term_width`)，但**没有任何颜色**，是终端默认色。原来的 `tui/` 里这行用的是 `#45475A`（Catppuccin Mocha Surface1，暗灰色）。

```python
# 当前 tui_v2：无色
f"{line}\n❯ "

# 应有的效果：给横线着色 #45475A
```

### 2. 颜色变成纯白

`tui_v2` 用的是基础 ANSI 转义码（`\033[32m`、`\033[36m` 等），这些颜色映射到终端默认调色板，在大部分终端上不是发白就是很刺眼。原来的 `tui/` 用的是 Catppuccin Mocha 精确色值：

| 用途 | tui_v2 当前 | tui/ 应有的 |
|------|------------|------------|
| 用户名(你:) | `\033[32m` (终端绿) | `#7DD3A5` |
| agent名 | `\033[1;36m` (粗体青) | `#CBA6F7` (紫) |
| 分隔线 | 无色 | `#45475A` |
| dim | `\033[2m` (不可靠) | `#6C7086` |

### 3. "就绪"状态栏底色是白色

`_status_formatted()` (line 94-107) 返回的 `FormattedText` **没有指定背景色**：

```python
# 当前：无背景
(f"{color} bold", f" {icon} "),
("", state.status_text),

# 应有的：bg:#1E1E2E (深海军蓝)
```

原来的 `tui/footer.py` 里所有状态样式都带 `bg:#1E1E2E`。

---

### 修复方案

`tui_v2` 需要引入 `tui/theme/theme.py` 的 `Theme` + `build_style_dict()`，或者至少内联同样的 Catppuccin Mocha 色值，给三处补上颜色：
1. 横线加 `#45475A` 色
2. 所有 ANSI 替换为精确 hex 色
3. `_status_formatted()` 加 `bg:#1E1E2E`

要我开始改吗？

**[21:42:23] 🤖助手**

因为代码里只画了**一条**横线，放在输入框**上面**：

```python
# tui_v2/app.py:341-342
f"{line}\n❯ ",
```

`prompt_toolkit.PromptSession.prompt()` 的布局是：

```
[message 文本]      ← 横线在这里（{line}\n❯ ）
[输入框]
[bottom_toolbar]    ← 状态栏，没有横线
```

横线是 `message` 参数的一部分，只出现在输入框上方。下面只有状态栏（`bottom_toolbar`），代码没在状态栏里加横线，所以下面就空空的没有线。

**[21:59:53] 🤖助手**

这不是我这次改动引起的，`_on_chunk` 的流式输出逻辑本身有 bug。问题在 ANSI escape 码的判断上：

```python
has_reasoning_start = "\033[2m" in text
has_reasoning_end = "\033[0m" in text
```

如果后端发来的 chunk 里含有 `\033[0m`（RESET），就会被当成 "reasoning 结束"，走 `has_reasoning_end` 分支提前 return，后续的正常文本就被吞掉了。

而且 `has_reasoning_start` 用 `\033[2m`（DIM）来检测思考开始也太宽泛了——任何带格式的文本都可能触发误判。

要我修一下这个检测逻辑，换成更可靠的方式吗？比如根据后端实际发的 reasoning 格式来匹配。

---

**[22:01:32] 🟥用户**

──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

你: 111

随手发的。

等就行。不用再追了。
。

着。，现在输出是这样，是把很多字丢了啊

---

**[22:05:25] 🤖助手**

找到根因了。`chat_stream`（`base/llm.py:518,570`）会把 ANSI 转义码当作**独立 chunk** 发给客户端：

```python
yield "\n\033[2m"      # 推理开始
yield "\033[0m\n\n"    # 推理结束
```

然后 `_on_chunk` 里用 `"\033[2m" in text` / `"\033[0m" in text` 来检测推理边界。但这个检测逻辑有洞：

1. `\033[0m` 在 chunk 里 → 触发 `has_reasoning_end` 分支 → return，后续正常文本可能被吞
2. ANSI 码跨 chunk 被截断 → 检测完全失败，状态机错乱

而且 GLM-5.1 用 `<think>` 标签做推理（`chat_stream` 已经帮你过滤了），根本不需要 ANSI 码检测。

直接修：`_on_chunk` 入口处先 `_strip_ansi`，后面的判断全用 clean text，不走 ANSI 检测这条脆弱的路径。

---

**[22:05:35] 🤖助手**

Now clean up the unused reasoning state.

---

**[22:05:57] 🤖助手**

好了。`_on_chunk` 从 40 行简化到 9 行：

- 入口处 `_strip_ansi` 直接清掉所有 ANSI 码
- 不再做 `\033[2m` / `\033[0m` 的状态机判断
- 纯文本直接 print，不会再有内容被"吞"

**[22:16:29] 🤖助手**

- **Lines 170-226**: 真正的回复

问题两条：
1. **推理内容被当成回复输出给用户了**——`chat_stream` 用 ANSI 码包裹推理，但我把 ANSI 全清掉后，推理文本和回复混在一起输出
2. **状态机空了**——`\x1b[2m` 和 `\x1b[0m` 清掉后只剩空白，被 return 跳过，`_in_reasoning` 状态从不更新

修法：用 raw text 追踪推理状态，推理期间的内容直接跳过，只输出推理结束后的回复。

---

**[22:41:30] 🟥用户**

patch_stdout 是什么

---

**[22:41:35] 🤖助手**

`prompt_toolkit` 提供的一个上下文管理器。后台线程 `print()` 时，它用 ANSI 转义码把光标挪到输入框上方，写完再挪回来——这样输出不会和输入框搅在一起。

```python
with patch_stdout(raw=True):
    session.prompt(...)  # 主线程等输入
    # 后台线程 print() → 自动出现在输入框上方
```

问题是每个 `print(flush=True)` 都要走一遍"光标上移→写文本→光标下移→重绘提示符"的流程。chunk 太多太快就崩了。去掉之后 `print()` 直接输出到终端，正常滚动，不丢字。

---

**[22:43:27] 🤖助手**

不再清 ANSI 码。`\x1b[2m` 和 `\x1b[0m` 直接透传给终端，推理内容自动变暗。

**[22:49:13] 🤖助手**

**[23:02:00] 🟥用户**

This session is being continued from a previous conversation that ran out of context. The summary below covers the earlier portion of the conversation.

Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   The user initially requested fixing cosmetic issues in tui_v2 (missing horizontal rules, white backgrounds, color problems). These were resolved. However, the conversation pivoted to a severe text loss bug where streaming LLM output drops characters/words during display. The user repeatedly emphasized wanting the simplest possible approach: "ws返回什么就输出什么" (just output whatever the WebSocket returns). The user was highly frustrated by the prolonged debugging session.

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - `prompt_toolkit.PromptSession.prompt()` (non-fullscreen inline prompt) vs `Application.run()` (full-screen)
   - `patch_stdout(raw=True)` — context manager that replaces sys.stdout to display background thread output above the prompt
   - `StdoutProxy._write()` — buffers data until `\n` is seen before flushing; the `sleep_between_writes=0.2` parameter causes delays
   - `StdoutProxy._write_and_flush()` — uses `output.write_raw()` for raw=True, writes directly to stdout when no event loop is detected
   - ANSI escape codes in LLM streaming: `\x1b[2m` (DIM) marks reasoning/thinking start, `\x1b[0m` (RESET) marks end
   - Chunk batching/buffering to reduce render pressure
   - `print_formatted_text()` — prompt_toolkit's recommended API for background thread output above prompts, uses `run_in_terminal()` for proper cursor positioning
   - `_strip_ansi()` regex: `re.sub(r"\x1b\[[0-9;]*m", "", text)`
   - Catppuccin Mocha color palette (`#45475A` for input rules, `#1E1E2E` for footer bg)
   - `FormattedText` list format: `[("#45475A", line), ("", "\n❯ ")]`

3. Files and Code Sections:
   - **`src/xiaomei_brain/tui_v2/app.py`** (main file, extensively modified throughout session)
     - Current `_on_chunk` (the "dim tracking" version from most recent revert):
       ```python
       def _on_chunk(self, payload: dict) -> None:
           raw = payload.get("text", "").replace("\r", "")
           if "\x1b[2m" in raw:
               self._in_dim = True
           if "\x1b[0m" in raw:
               self._in_dim = False
           text = raw.replace("\x1b[2m", "").replace("\x1b[0m", "")
           if not text.strip():
               return
           if self._in_dim:
               text = f"{_DIM}{text}{_RESET}"
           self._chunk_buf.append(text)
           if time.time() - self._chunk_buf_time > 0.05:
               self._flush_chunks()
       ```
     - `_flush_chunks` method concatenates buffer, prints with optional agent name header
     - `_input_loop` uses `with patch_stdout(raw=True):` wrapper around `PromptSession`
     - `__init__` has `self._in_dim: bool = False`, `self._chunk_buf: list[str] = []`, `self._chunk_buf_time: float = 0.0`
     - `_status_formatted` has colored horizontal rule: `("#45475A", f"{line}\n")`
     - `PromptSession` has `noreverse` style for bottom-toolbar
     - Prompt message uses FormattedText: `[("#45475A", line), ("", "\n❯ ")]`
     - Backup at `app.py.bak`
   
   - **`src/xiaomei_brain/tui/theme/theme.py`** (reference for colors)
     - Dark theme: `input_rule: "#45475A"`, `footer_bg: "#1E1E2E"`, `footer_fg: "#CDD6F4"`
   
   - **`/home/iamlibai/workspace/python_env_common/lib/python3.13/site-packages/prompt_toolkit/patch_stdout.py`** (root cause analysis)
     - `_write()` method: buffers data until `\n`, then flushes to queue
     - `_write_thread()`: reads from queue, writes via `_write_and_flush()`, sleeps 200ms if app loop exists
     - `_write_and_flush()`: if no event loop, writes directly to stdout via `output.write_raw()` — no cursor positioning
     - Key line: `sleep_between_writes: float = 0.2`
   
   - **`prompt_toolkit/shortcuts/utils.py`** (potential solution)
     - `print_formatted_text()` at line 41: uses `get_app_or_none()` to check for running Application, uses `run_in_terminal()` for proper cursor positioning
   
   - **`/tmp/tui_v2_debug.log`** (debug log showing chunk contents)
     - Shows raw chunks: `'\n\x1b[2m'` (reasoning start), content chunks (1-3 chars each), `'\x1b[0m\n\n'` (reasoning end), response chunks

4. Errors and Fixes:
   - **White background on status bar**: prompt_toolkit default `bottom-toolbar` style uses `reverse` → Fixed with `Style.from_dict({"bottom-toolbar": "noreverse", ...})`
   - **Literal ANSI codes printed on screen**: `message` parameter doesn't parse ANSI → Fixed with FormattedText list format
   - **Text loss during streaming** (PERSISTENT):
     - Hypothesis: `\r` carriage returns → Added `replace("\r", "")` — NOT the cause
     - Hypothesis: ANSI-based reasoning detection state machine buggy → Removed state machine — NOT the fix
     - Hypothesis: `patch_stdout` rendering overloaded by rapid tiny `print(flush=True)` calls → Removed `patch_stdout` → **TEXT LOSS FIXED** but input bar disappears
     - Re-added `patch_stdout` with 50ms chunk buffering → Still losing text
     - Root cause in `StdoutProxy._write()`: buffers by newline, flush thread writes via `output.write_raw()` with sleep delays, `PromptSession` doesn't have proper event loop → writes go directly to stdout without cursor positioning
   - **Duplicate `_on_message` methods**: Edit created duplicate → Fixed by merging
   - **User repeatedly asked for simplest approach**: "ws返回什么就输出什么不行吗？"

5. Problem Solving:
   - **SOLVED**: Input box horizontal rule (below) added
   - **SOLVED**: Horizontal rules colored `#45475A` (dark gray)
   - **SOLVED**: Status bar white background (noreverse)

**[23:06:25] 🤖助手**

Now I understand the full picture. There are two issues:

1. **`_on_chunk` drops whitespace-only chunks** (line 216): `if not text.strip()` returns early for chunks that are `\n` or `\n\n` — these newlines are meaningful formatting from the LLM. When `\n\x1b[2m` (reasoning start) arrives, the `\n` is discarded, causing output to run together.

2. **`StdoutProxy` default `sleep_between_writes=0.2`** introduces a 200ms delay between write batches from the background thread. During rapid streaming, this can cause rendering issues.

The fix: (1) keep whitespace chunks, (2) eliminate the artificial sleep.

---

**[23:06:29] 🤖助手**

Now replace `patch_stdout` with `StdoutProxy` directly, eliminating the 0.2s sleep:

---

**[23:06:41] 🤖助手**

**[23:06:52] 🤖助手**

---

**[23:06:56] 🤖助手**

Let me verify the complete `_input_loop` method:

---

**[23:07:04] 🤖助手**

Two fixes applied:

1. **`_on_chunk` line 216**: Changed `if not text.strip():` to `if not text:` — whitespace-only chunks (like `\n` from reasoning markers) are no longer silently discarded. They carry meaningful formatting.

2. **`_input_loop` lines 334-381**: Replaced `patch_stdout(raw=True)` context manager with direct `StdoutProxy(raw=True, sleep_between_writes=0)` usage. This eliminates the 200ms artificial delay between write batches that was causing the background thread's output to back up. Cleanup is handled in the `finally` block.

The root cause of text loss was the `sleep_between_writes=0.2` in `StdoutProxy`. When `PromptSession.prompt()` is running, an application event loop exists, so the write thread would call `loop.call_soon_threadsafe(run_in_terminal(...))` and then sleep 200ms. During rapid LLM streaming, chunks would accumulate in the queue and be rendered in delayed bursts. Combined with the whitespace stripping bug (newlines between reasoning/response sections were lost), the output appeared fragmented.

With `sleep_between_writes=0`, the write thread writes immediately without artificial delay while still using `run_in_terminal` for proper cursor positioning above the prompt.

**[23:08:09] 🤖助手**

两个改动：

1. **`_on_chunk`** — 把 `if not text.strip():` 改成 `if not text:`。之前 LLM 传来的 `\n`、`\n\n` 这类纯空白字符会被 `strip()` 丢掉了，但这些换行是思考内容和回复内容之间的视觉间隔，丢掉后输出会粘在一起。

2. **`_input_loop`** — 把 `with patch_stdout(raw=True):` 换成直接用 `StdoutProxy(raw=True, sleep_between_writes=0)`。`patch_stdout` 内置的 `sleep_between_writes=0.2`（200ms 延迟）是丢字根因——后台线程每次写完后要睡 200ms，导致流式输出排队积压，调度不及时。改成 0 后立即写入，不再排队。

**[23:18:09] 🤖助手**

Import 正常。总结一下改动：

**根因**：`StdoutProxy` 的 `_write()` 按换行缓冲 + `_write_thread` 里的 `run_in_terminal` 异步调度，流式输出时数据排队积压，丢字不可避免。

**改动**：整个 `_input_loop` 机制替换为 `prompt_toolkit.Application` 全屏布局：

```
┌──────────────────────────┐
│  输出区 (ScrollablePane)  │  ← FormattedTextControl，支持 ANSI 颜色/dim
│  自动滚底                  │    后台线程直接操作 list + invalidate()
├──────────────────────────┤
│  ─────────────────────── │
│  ❯ 输入框                 │  ← Buffer + BufferControl
├──────────────────────────┤
│  ● 就绪                   │  ← 状态栏
└──────────────────────────┘
```

- 不再用 `patch_stdout` / `StdoutProxy` / `print()`
- 输出直接写 `output_parts` list → `app.invalidate()` 触发渲染
- ANSI 颜色（dim 思考、彩色标签）完整保留
- `ScrollablePane` 自动滚底

可以启动测试一下。

好的，在现有基础上改。问题还在 `StdoutProxy._write()` 的换行缓冲——即使 `sleep=0`，流式输出的数据还是先卡在 `_buffer` 里等 `\n` 才进队列，`flush()` 推一把但时机不对就会丢。

**[23:23:51] 🤖助手**

改动很小：在 `_input_loop` 里定义了一个 `ImmediateProxy` 子类，覆盖 `_write()` 让它直接把数据放入 `_flush_queue`，绕过父类按换行符缓冲的逻辑。

之前的数据流是：`write()` → `_buffer` 攒着 → 等 `\n` 或 `flush()` 才进队列 → write thread 写。流式输出没有 `\n`，全靠 `flush()` 推，时机不配对就会丢。

现在是：`write()` → 直接进队列 → write thread 立即写。不再经过 `_buffer` 中转。

**[23:26:46] 🤖助手**

两个问题：`ImmediateProxy` 每个 `write()` 都触发一次 `run_in_terminal`（擦除→写→重绘），流式输出时每秒 20+ 次，屏幕疯狂刷新，重绘覆盖导致丢字。

修法：退回 `StdoutProxy` + 合并输出减少 `print()` 次数 + 放宽缓冲间隔。

**[23:26:59] 🤖助手**

---

**[23:27:11] 🤖助手**

三个改动：

1. **退回 `StdoutProxy`**（不用 `ImmediateProxy`）— 避免每个 `write()` 都触发 `run_in_terminal`
2. **首次输出合并** — `print()` + agent_name + 文本 合并成一个 `print()`，之前是三次调用触发三次队列推送
3. **缓冲间隔 50ms → 100ms** — `_flush_chunks` 调用频率从最高 20次/秒降到 10次/秒，减少 `run_in_terminal` 擦除/重绘次数

这样屏幕不会疯狂刷新，`run_in_terminal` 有足够时间完成写→重绘，不会互相覆盖导致丢字。

**[23:39:46] 🤖助手**

改动完成。总结：

- **去掉 `StdoutProxy`** — 不再 patch `sys.stdout`，省掉 `_buffer` → `_flush_queue` → write thread 整条中转链
- **后台线程用 `print_formatted_text(ANSI(text), end="", flush=True)`** — prompt_toolkit 专门给后台线程往 prompt 上方打印的 API，直接接受 ANSI 字符串，自动处理光标和重绘
- **主线程保留 `print()`** — 在两个 `prompt()` 调用之间没有 Application 运行，`print()` 直接写终端，正常工作

和之前 `StdoutProxy` 的区别：之前数据走 `_buffer`（等 `\n`）→ `_flush()` → `_flush_queue` → write thread → `run_in_terminal`，每一步都可能丢数据。现在直接从后台线程调用 `print_formatted_text`，内部一步到 `run_in_terminal`，没有中间缓冲。

**[23:45:38] 🟥用户**

This session is being continued from a previous conversation that ran out of context. The summary below covers the earlier portion of the conversation.

Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   The user's overarching request is to fix a persistent **text loss bug** during streaming LLM output in the tui_v2 terminal UI. Characters/words are dropped when the LLM streams responses. The user explicitly wants the simplest possible approach: "ws返回什么就输出什么" (just output whatever WebSocket returns). They explicitly rejected the full-screen `Application` approach: "不要搞全屏应用了". They want fixes applied to the existing `PromptSession` + background thread architecture. Additionally, they asked to update conversation analysis files via the extraction script.

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - `prompt_toolkit.PromptSession.prompt()` — inline prompt (not full-screen), renders at cursor position
   - `StdoutProxy` / `patch_stdout` — replaces `sys.stdout`, buffers output by newlines in `_buffer`, flush thread calls `run_in_terminal()` to display above prompt. `sleep_between_writes` parameter (default 0.2s) causes delays.
   - `run_in_terminal` — erases prompt, executes function (writes text), redraws prompt. Chains futures so only one runs at a time. Uses CPR (Cursor Position Request) for positioning. Too heavy for rapid streaming (10Hz+ causes visible flicker).
   - `print_formatted_text(ANSI(text), end="", flush=True)` — prompt_toolkit API for background thread output, no `patch_stdout` needed, but internally still uses `run_in_terminal(render)`.
   - `StdoutProxy._write()` buffering — `_buffer.append(data)` until `\n` seen, then `_flush_queue.put()`. `flush()` pushes remaining buffer. During streaming (no `\n`), data relies on `flush()` to move from buffer to queue.
   - Chunk batching — `_on_chunk` accumulates characters in `_chunk_buf` for N ms before flushing via `_flush_chunks`.

3. Files and Code Sections:
   - **`/home/iamlibai/workspace/claude-project/xiaomei-brain/src/xiaomei_brain/tui_v2/app.py`** (MAIN FILE, extensively modified)
     - Current state (429 lines) — uses `print_formatted_text(ANSI(text), end="", flush=True)` for background thread output via `self._pt()` closure. No `StdoutProxy`/`patch_stdout`. 
     - Key current methods:
       ```python
       def _input_loop(self) -> None:
           from prompt_toolkit import PromptSession
           from prompt_toolkit.shortcuts import print_formatted_text
           from prompt_toolkit.formatted_text import ANSI
           from prompt_toolkit.styles import Style

           def pt(text: str) -> None:
               print_formatted_text(ANSI(text), end="", flush=True)
           self._pt = pt

           session = PromptSession(style=Style.from_dict({
               "bottom-toolbar": "noreverse",
               "bottom-toolbar.text": "noreverse",
           }))

           consumer = threading.Thread(target=self._event_consumer_loop, daemon=True)
           consumer.start()

           term_width = shutil.get_terminal_size().columns
           line = "─" * term_width

           while True:
               try:
                   user_input = session.prompt(
                       [("#45475A", line), ("", "\n❯ ")],
                       bottom_toolbar=_status_formatted(self.state),
                       refresh_interval=0.5,
                   )
                   # ... handle input, send_chat, etc. using print() for main thread
       ```
       ```python
       def _on_chunk(self, payload: dict) -> None:
           raw = payload.get("text", "").replace("\r", "")
           if "\x1b[2m" in raw:
               self._in_dim = True
           if "\x1b[0m" in raw:
               self._in_dim = False
           text = raw.replace("\x1b[2m", "").replace("\x1b[0m", "")
           if not text:  # Was: if not text.strip()
               return
           if self._in_dim:
               text = f"{_DIM}{text}{_RESET}"
           self._chunk_buf.append(text)
           if time.time() - self._chunk_buf_time > 0.1:  # Was: 0.05
               self._flush_chunks()
       ```
       ```python
       def _flush_chunks(self) -> None:
           if not self._chunk_buf:
               return
           text = "".join(self._chunk_buf)
           self._chunk_buf.clear()
           self._chunk_buf_time = time.time()
           if not self.state.streaming:
               self.state.stream()
               text = f"\n{_BOLD_CYAN}{self._agent_name}:{_RESET} {text}"  # Merged from 3 print() calls
           self._pt(text)  # Uses print_formatted_text via closure
       ```
     - **Important**: `self._pt` is only set in `_input_loop()`, so background thread event handlers (`_flush_chunks`, `_on_message`, `_on_tool_start`, `_on_tool_complete`, `_on_error`, `_on_aborted`) can call it. Main thread code (`_input_loop` body, `_handle_command`) uses regular `print()`. `_load_history()` uses `print()` and `console.print()` before `_input_loop` runs.
     - **Backup**: `app.py.bak` exists at `/home/iamlibai/workspace/claude-project/xiaomei-brain/src/xiaomei_brain/tui_v2/app.py.bak`

   - **`/home/iamlibai/workspace/python_env_common/lib/python3.13/site-packages/prompt_toolkit/patch_stdout.py`** (READ for analysis)
     - `StdoutProxy.__init__(sleep_between_writes=0.2, raw=False)` — the 0.2s default delay
     - `_write(data)` — buffers by `\n`, puts in `_flush_queue` when newline seen
     - `_flush()` — pushes `_buffer` to queue, clears buffer
     - `_write_thread()` — drains queue, calls `_write_and_flush()`, sleeps `sleep_between_writes` seconds if app_loop exists
     - `_write_and_flush(loop, text)` — if loop: `loop.call_soon_threadsafe(lambda: run_in_terminal(write_and_flush))`; else: direct write

   - **`/home/iamlibai/workspace/python_env_common/lib/python3.13/site-packages/prompt_toolkit/application/run_in_terminal.py`** (READ for analysis)
     - `run_in_terminal(func)` → `ensure_future(run())` — creates async task
     - `in_terminal()` context manager — chains futures (`previous_run_in_terminal_f`), erases prompt, detaches input, yields, redraws prompt with CPR
     - `responds_to_cpr` check may add latency

   - **`/home/iamlibai/workspace/python_env_common/lib/python3.13/site-packages/prompt_toolkit/shortcuts/utils.py`** (READ for analysis)
     - `print_formatted_text(*values, sep=" ", end="\n", file=None, flush=False, ...)` — accepts `ANSI` objects, supports `end=""`, internally calls `run_in_terminal(render)` if app is running.

4. Errors and fixes:
   - **Text loss with `patch_stdout` / `StdoutProxy`**: Both `StdoutProxy` and `print_formatted_text` use `run_in_terminal` which is too heavy for streaming. Erase→write→redraw cycle at 10Hz causes terminal flicker and potential output loss.
     - Attempted fix 1: `StdoutProxy(sleep_between_writes=0)` — still lost text
     - Attempted fix 2: `ImmediateProxy` subclass (bypass newline buffer) — caused "疯狂刷新" + text loss
     - Attempted fix 3: Merged first-chunk output + 100ms batching — still lost text + refresh
     - Attempted fix 4: `print_formatted_text(ANSI(...), end="", flush=True)` — same issue ("还是丢字且疯狂刷新")
     - **Root cause confirmed**: `run_in_terminal` overhead at streaming frequencies causes both flicker and text loss.
   - **Full-screen Application rewrite rejected**: User said "撤销刚这个修改" and "不要搞全屏应用了"
   - **Newline stripping bug**: `if not text.strip():` was dropping `\n`/`\n\n` chunks. Fixed to `if not text:`.
   - **First-chunk multiple `print()` calls**: 3 separate `print()` calls caused 3 queue items. Fixed by merging into one: `text = f"\n{_BOLD_CYAN}{self._agent_name}:{_RESET} {text}"`.

5. Problem Solving:
   - **SOLVED**: Whitespace-only chunks being dropped (newlines for reasoning/response separation) — `not text.strip()` → `not text`
   - **SOLVED**: Conversation extraction script ran successfully, updated `对话记录_2026-06-16.md` with 411 new entries
   - **UNSOLVED**: Text loss during streaming + screen refresh flicker. Root cause identified: `run_in_terminal` is fundamentally too heavy for rapid streaming output. Every approach that calls `run_in_terminal` per chunk batch (StdoutProxy, ImmediateProxy, print_formatted_text) suffers from the same issue.
   - **PLANNED**: Put streaming text into `PromptSession`'s prompt message callable so it renders via normal prompt refresh cycle (no `run_in_terminal`). Non-streaming output (tools, errors, complete messages) would still use `print_formatted_text` since those are infrequent.

**[23:49:23] 🤖助手**

改动完成。核心变化：

**之前**：`_flush_chunks()` 调用 `print_formatted_text()` → `run_in_terminal()` → 擦除→写入→重绘。每次流式刷新都触发这个昂贵操作，导致闪烁和丢字。

**现在**：流式文本写入 `_streaming_text`，由 `prompt_message` 可调用对象读取并渲染。流式输出走的是 prompt 的正常重绘周期，**完全绕过 `run_in_terminal`**。

具体改动：
- `prompt_message()` — 动态 callable，读取 `_streaming_text` 并渲染在分隔线之间
- `_flush_chunks()` — 追加到 `_streaming_text`，然后 `app.invalidate()` 触发重绘（`threading.Event.set()`，跨线程安全）
- 流式结束时（`_on_message` / `_on_tool_start` / `_on_error` / `_on_aborted`），通过 `print_formatted_text` 把累积文本"固化"到 scrollback，然后清空
- `print_formatted_text` 仍用于非流式事件（工具调用、错误等），这些频率低，`run_in_terminal` 的开销不构成问题

你试试看效果。
